          <td id="L493" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="493"></td>
          <td id="LC493" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Build GDB with GNU MPFR, a library for multiple-precision</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L494" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="494"></td>
          <td id="LC494" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     floating-point computation with correct rounding.  (Done by</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L495" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="495"></td>
          <td id="LC495" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     default if GNU MPFR is installed and found at configure time.)</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L496" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="496"></td>
          <td id="LC496" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     This library is used to emulate target floating-point arithmetic</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L497" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="497"></td>
          <td id="LC497" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     during expression evaluation when the target uses different</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L498" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="498"></td>
          <td id="LC498" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     floating-point formats than the host.  If GNU MPFR is not</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L499" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="499"></td>
          <td id="LC499" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     available, GDB will fall back to using host floating-point</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L500" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="500"></td>
          <td id="LC500" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     arithmetic.  If your host does not have GNU MPFR installed, you</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L501" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="501"></td>
          <td id="LC501" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     can get the latest version from `https://www.mpfr.org/&#39;.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L502" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="502"></td>
          <td id="LC502" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L503" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="503"></td>
          <td id="LC503" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--with-python[=PYTHON]&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L504" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="504"></td>
          <td id="LC504" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Build GDB with Python scripting support.  (Done by default if</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L505" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="505"></td>
          <td id="LC505" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     libpython is present and found at configure time.)  Python makes</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L506" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="506"></td>
          <td id="LC506" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     GDB scripting much more powerful than the restricted CLI</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L507" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="507"></td>
          <td id="LC507" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     scripting language.  If your host does not have Python installed,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L508" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="508"></td>
          <td id="LC508" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     you can find it on `http://www.python.org/download/&#39;.  The oldest</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L509" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="509"></td>
          <td id="LC509" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     version of Python supported by GDB is 2.6.  The optional argument</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L510" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="510"></td>
          <td id="LC510" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     PYTHON is used to find the Python headers and libraries.  It can</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L511" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="511"></td>
          <td id="LC511" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     be either the name of a Python executable, or the name of the</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L512" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="512"></td>
          <td id="LC512" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     directory in which Python is installed.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L513" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="513"></td>
          <td id="LC513" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L514" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="514"></td>
          <td id="LC514" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--with-guile[=GUILE]&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L515" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="515"></td>
          <td id="LC515" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Build GDB with GNU Guile scripting support.  (Done by default if</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L516" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="516"></td>
          <td id="LC516" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     libguile is present and found at configure time.)  If your host</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L517" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="517"></td>
          <td id="LC517" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     does not have Guile installed, you can find it at</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L518" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="518"></td>
          <td id="LC518" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     `https://www.gnu.org/software/guile/&#39;.  The optional argument</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L519" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="519"></td>
          <td id="LC519" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     GUILE can be a version number, which will cause `configure&#39; to</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L520" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="520"></td>
          <td id="LC520" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     try to use that version of Guile; or the file name of a</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L521" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="521"></td>
          <td id="LC521" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     `pkg-config&#39; executable, which will be queried to find the</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L522" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="522"></td>
          <td id="LC522" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     information needed to compile and link against Guile.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L523" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="523"></td>
          <td id="LC523" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L524" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="524"></td>
          <td id="LC524" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--enable-source-highlight&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L525" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="525"></td>
          <td id="LC525" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     When printing source code, use source highlighting.  This requires</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>

</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L529" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="529"></td>
          <td id="LC529" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--with-xxhash&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L530" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="530"></td>
          <td id="LC530" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Use libxxhash for hashing.  This has no user-visible effect but</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L531" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="531"></td>

</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L534" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="534"></td>
          <td id="LC534" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--without-included-regex&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L535" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="535"></td>
          <td id="LC535" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Don&#39;t use the regex library included with GDB (as part of the</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L536" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="536"></td>

          <td id="LC539" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--with-sysroot=DIR&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L540" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="540"></td>
          <td id="LC540" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Use DIR as the default system root directory for libraries whose</td>

          <td id="L541" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="541"></td>

        </tr>

          <td id="L544" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="544"></td>
          <td id="LC544" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     `--exec-prefix&#39; options), the default system root will be</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L545" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="545"></td>
          <td id="LC545" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     automatically adjusted if and when GDB is moved to a different</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L546" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="546"></td>
          <td id="LC546" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     location.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L547" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="547"></td>
          <td id="LC547" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L548" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="548"></td>
          <td id="LC548" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--with-system-gdbinit=FILE&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L549" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="549"></td>
          <td id="LC549" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Configure GDB to automatically load a system-wide init file.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L550" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="550"></td>
          <td id="LC550" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     FILE should be an absolute file name.  If FILE is in a directory</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L551" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="551"></td>
          <td id="LC551" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     under the configured prefix, and GDB is moved to another location</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L552" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="552"></td>
          <td id="LC552" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     after being built, the location of the system-wide init file will</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L553" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="553"></td>
          <td id="LC553" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     be adjusted accordingly. </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L554" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="554"></td>
          <td id="LC554" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L555" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="555"></td>
          <td id="LC555" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--with-system-gdbinit-dir=DIR&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L556" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="556"></td>
          <td id="LC556" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Configure GDB to automatically load system-wide init files from</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L557" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="557"></td>
          <td id="LC557" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     a directory. Files with extensions `.gdb&#39;, `.py&#39; (if Python</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L558" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="558"></td>
          <td id="LC558" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     support is enabled) and `.scm&#39; (if Guile support is enabled) are</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L559" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="559"></td>
          <td id="LC559" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     supported.  DIR should be an absolute directory name.  If DIR is</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L560" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="560"></td>
          <td id="LC560" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     in a directory under the configured prefix, and GDB is moved to</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L561" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="561"></td>
          <td id="LC561" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     another location after being built, the location of the system-</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L562" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="562"></td>
          <td id="LC562" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     wide init directory will be adjusted accordingly.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L563" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="563"></td>
          <td id="LC563" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L564" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="564"></td>
          <td id="LC564" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--enable-build-warnings&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L565" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="565"></td>
          <td id="LC565" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     When building the GDB sources, ask the compiler to warn about any</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L566" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="566"></td>
          <td id="LC566" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     code which looks even vaguely suspicious.  It passes many</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L567" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="567"></td>
          <td id="LC567" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     different warning flags, depending on the exact version of the</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L568" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="568"></td>
          <td id="LC568" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     compiler you are using.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L569" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="569"></td>
          <td id="LC569" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L570" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="570"></td>
          <td id="LC570" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--enable-werror&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L571" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="571"></td>
          <td id="LC571" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Treat compiler warnings as werrors.  It adds the -Werror flag to</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L572" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="572"></td>
          <td id="LC572" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     the compiler, which will fail the compilation if the compiler</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L573" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="573"></td>
          <td id="LC573" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     outputs any warning messages.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L574" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="574"></td>
          <td id="LC574" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L575" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="575"></td>
          <td id="LC575" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--enable-ubsan&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L576" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="576"></td>
          <td id="LC576" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Enable the GCC undefined behavior sanitizer.  By default this is</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L577" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="577"></td>
          <td id="LC577" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     disabled in GDB releases, but enabled when building from git.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L578" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="578"></td>
          <td id="LC578" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     The undefined behavior sanitizer checks for C++ undefined</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L579" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="579"></td>
          <td id="LC579" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     behavior.  It has a performance cost, so if you are looking at</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L580" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="580"></td>
          <td id="LC580" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     GDB&#39;s performance, you should disable it.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L581" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="581"></td>
          <td id="LC581" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L582" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="582"></td>
          <td id="LC582" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`--enable-unit-tests[=yes|no]&#39;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L583" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="583"></td>
          <td id="LC583" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     Enable (i.e., include) support for unit tests when compiling GDB</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L584" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="584"></td>
          <td id="LC584" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     and GDBServer.  Note that if this option is not passed, GDB will</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L585" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="585"></td>
          <td id="LC585" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     have selftests if it is a development build, and will *not* have</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L586" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="586"></td>
          <td id="LC586" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     selftests if it is a non-development build.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L587" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="587"></td>
          <td id="LC587" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L588" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="588"></td>
          <td id="LC588" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`configure&#39; accepts other options, for compatibility with configuring</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L589" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="589"></td>
          <td id="LC589" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">other GNU tools recursively.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L590" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="590"></td>
          <td id="LC590" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L591" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="591"></td>
          <td id="LC591" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L592" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="592"></td>
          <td id="LC592" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Remote debugging</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L593" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="593"></td>
          <td id="LC593" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">=================</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L594" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="594"></td>
          <td id="LC594" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L595" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="595"></td>
          <td id="LC595" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   The files m68k-stub.c, i386-stub.c, and sparc-stub.c are examples</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L596" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="596"></td>
          <td id="LC596" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">of remote stubs to be used with remote.c.  They are designed to run</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L597" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="597"></td>
          <td id="LC597" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">standalone on an m68k, i386, or SPARC cpu and communicate properly</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L598" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="598"></td>
          <td id="LC598" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">with the remote.c stub over a serial line.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L599" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="599"></td>
          <td id="LC599" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L600" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="600"></td>
          <td id="LC600" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   The directory gdbserver/ contains `gdbserver&#39;, a program that</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L601" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="601"></td>
          <td id="LC601" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">allows remote debugging for Unix applications.  GDBserver is only</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L602" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="602"></td>
          <td id="LC602" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">supported for some native configurations.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L603" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="603"></td>
          <td id="LC603" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L604" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="604"></td>
          <td id="LC604" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   The file gdbserver/README includes further notes on GDBserver; in</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L605" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="605"></td>
          <td id="LC605" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">particular, it explains how to build GDBserver for cross-debugging</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L606" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="606"></td>
          <td id="LC606" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(where GDBserver runs on the target machine, which is of a different</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L607" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="607"></td>
          <td id="LC607" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">architecture than the host machine running GDB).</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L608" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="608"></td>
          <td id="LC608" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L609" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="609"></td>
          <td id="LC609" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L610" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="610"></td>
          <td id="LC610" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Reporting Bugs in GDB</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L611" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="611"></td>
          <td id="LC611" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">=====================</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L612" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="612"></td>
          <td id="LC612" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L613" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="613"></td>
          <td id="LC613" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   There are several ways of reporting bugs in GDB.  The prefered</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L614" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="614"></td>
          <td id="LC614" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">method is to use the World Wide Web:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L615" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="615"></td>
          <td id="LC615" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L616" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="616"></td>
          <td id="LC616" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">      http://www.gnu.org/software/gdb/bugs/</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L617" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="617"></td>
          <td id="LC617" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L618" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="618"></td>
          <td id="LC618" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">As an alternative, the bug report can be submitted, via e-mail, to the</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L619" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="619"></td>
          <td id="LC619" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">address &quot;bug-gdb@gnu.org&quot;.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L620" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="620"></td>
          <td id="LC620" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L621" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="621"></td>
          <td id="LC621" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   When submitting a bug, please include the GDB version number, and</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L622" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="622"></td>
          <td id="LC622" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">how you configured it (e.g., &quot;sun4&quot; or &quot;mach386 host,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L623" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="623"></td>
          <td id="LC623" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">i586-intel-synopsys target&quot;).  Since GDB supports so many</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L624" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="624"></td>
          <td id="LC624" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">different configurations, it is important that you be precise about</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L625" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="625"></td>
          <td id="LC625" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">this.  The simplest way to do this is to include the output from these</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L626" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="626"></td>
          <td id="LC626" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">commands:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L627" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="627"></td>

</td>
        </tr>

          <td id="LC667" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">GDB Testsuite</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L668" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="668"></td>
          <td id="LC668" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">=============</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L669" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="669"></td>
          <td id="LC669" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L670" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="670"></td>
          <td id="LC670" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   Included with the GDB distribution is a DejaGNU based testsuite</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L671" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="671"></td>
          <td id="LC671" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">that can either be used to test your newly built GDB, or for</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L672" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="672"></td>
          <td id="LC672" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">regression testing a GDB with local modifications.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L673" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="673"></td>
          <td id="LC673" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L674" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="674"></td>
          <td id="LC674" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   Running the testsuite requires the prior installation of DejaGNU,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L675" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="675"></td>
          <td id="LC675" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">which is generally available via ftp.  The directory</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L676" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="676"></td>
          <td id="LC676" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">ftp://sources.redhat.com/pub/dejagnu/ will contain a recent snapshot.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L677" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="677"></td>
          <td id="LC677" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Once DejaGNU is installed, you can run the tests in one of the</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L678" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="678"></td>
          <td id="LC678" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">following ways:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L679" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="679"></td>
          <td id="LC679" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L680" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="680"></td>
          <td id="LC680" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  (1)	cd gdb-VERSION</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L681" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="681"></td>
          <td id="LC681" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	make check-gdb</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L682" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="682"></td>
          <td id="LC682" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L683" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="683"></td>
          <td id="LC683" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">or</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L684" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="684"></td>
          <td id="LC684" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L685" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="685"></td>
          <td id="LC685" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  (2)	cd gdb-VERSION/gdb</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L686" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="686"></td>
          <td id="LC686" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	make check</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L687" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="687"></td>
          <td id="LC687" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L688" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="688"></td>
          <td id="LC688" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">or</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L689" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="689"></td>
          <td id="LC689" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L690" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="690"></td>
          <td id="LC690" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  (3)	cd gdb-VERSION/gdb/testsuite</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L691" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="691"></td>
          <td id="LC691" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	make site.exp	(builds the site specific file)</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L692" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="692"></td>
          <td id="LC692" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	runtest -tool gdb GDB=../gdb    (or GDB=&lt;somepath&gt; as appropriate)</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L693" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="693"></td>
          <td id="LC693" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L694" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="694"></td>
          <td id="LC694" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When using a `make&#39;-based method, you can use the Makefile variable</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L695" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="695"></td>
          <td id="LC695" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`RUNTESTFLAGS&#39; to pass flags to `runtest&#39;, e.g.:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L696" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="696"></td>
          <td id="LC696" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L697" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="697"></td>
          <td id="LC697" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">	make RUNTESTFLAGS=--directory=gdb.cp check</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L698" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="698"></td>
          <td id="LC698" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L699" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="699"></td>
          <td id="LC699" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">If you use GNU make, you can use its `-j&#39; option to run the testsuite</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L700" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="700"></td>
          <td id="LC700" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">in parallel.  This can greatly reduce the amount of time it takes for</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L701" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="701"></td>
          <td id="LC701" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the testsuite to run.  In this case, if you set `RUNTESTFLAGS&#39; then,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L702" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="702"></td>
          <td id="LC702" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">by default, the tests will be run serially even under `-j&#39;.  You can</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L703" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="703"></td>
          <td id="LC703" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">override this and force a parallel run by setting the `make&#39; variable</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L704" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="704"></td>
          <td id="LC704" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">`FORCE_PARALLEL&#39; to any non-empty value.  Note that the parallel `make</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L705" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="705"></td>
          <td id="LC705" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">check&#39; assumes that you want to run the entire testsuite, so it is not</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L706" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="706"></td>
          <td id="LC706" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">compatible with some dejagnu options, like `--directory&#39;.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L707" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="707"></td>
          <td id="LC707" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L708" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="708"></td>
          <td id="LC708" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The last method gives you slightly more control in case of problems</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L709" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="709"></td>
          <td id="LC709" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">with building one or more test executables or if you are using the</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L710" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="710"></td>
          <td id="LC710" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">testsuite `standalone&#39;, without it being part of the GDB source tree.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L711" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="711"></td>
          <td id="LC711" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L712" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="712"></td>
          <td id="LC712" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">See the DejaGNU documentation for further details.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L713" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="713"></td>
          <td id="LC713" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L714" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="714"></td>
          <td id="LC714" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L715" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="715"></td>
          <td id="LC715" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Copyright and License Notices</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L716" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="716"></td>
          <td id="LC716" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">=============================</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L717" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="717"></td>

</td>

          <td id="LC721" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To reduce the length of copyright notices, consecutive years in the</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L722" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="722"></td>
          <td id="LC722" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">copyright notice can be combined into a single range.  For instance,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L723" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="723"></td>

        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L724" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="724"></td>

</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L725" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="725"></td>
          <td id="LC725" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    1986, 1988, 1989, 1991-1993, 1999, 2000, 2007, 2008, 2009, 2010, 2011</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L726" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="726"></td>

</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L727" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="727"></td>
          <td id="LC727" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">... is abbreviated into:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L728" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number" data-line-number="728"></td>
          <td id="LC728" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
